    { 5358;1   ;DataItem;ConsolidatedBalances;
               DataItemTable=Table2000000026;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(Number)
                                 WHERE(Number=FILTER(1));
               OnAfterGetRecord=VAR
                                  TotalServTaxPaymentDetails@1500001 : Record 16477;
                                  TotalSTAsExciseUtilization@1500002 : Record 16570;
                                BEGIN
                                  // Openning Balance
                                  CalcTaxInPeriod(0D,StartDate - 1,OpeningBalance,OpeningBalanceEcess,OpeningBalanceSheCess,OpeningBalanceKKCess);

                                  CalcTaxPaymentsInPeriod(0D,StartDate - 1,TotalServTaxPaymentDetails);
                                  OpeningBalance -= TotalServTaxPaymentDetails."Credit availed";
                                  OpeningBalanceEcess -= TotalServTaxPaymentDetails."Credit availed (eCess)";
                                  OpeningBalanceSheCess -= TotalServTaxPaymentDetails."Credit availed (SHECess)";
                                  OpeningBalanceKKCess -= TotalServTaxPaymentDetails."Credit Available (KKC)";

                                  CalcExcisePaidInPeriod(0D,StartDate - 1,TotalSTAsExciseUtilization);
                                  OpeningBalance -= TotalSTAsExciseUtilization."ST as Excise Utilisation";
                                  OpeningBalanceEcess -= TotalSTAsExciseUtilization."ST eCess as Excise Utilisation";
                                  OpeningBalanceSheCess -= TotalSTAsExciseUtilization."ST SHECess Excise Utilisation";

                                  // Reporting period
                                  CalcTaxInPeriod(StartDate,EndDate,CreditAvailed,CreditAvailedECess,CreditAvailedSHECess,CreditAvailedKKCess);

                                  CalcTaxPaymentsInPeriod(StartDate,EndDate,TotalServTaxPaymentDetails);
                                  CreditUsedForSTPmt := TotalServTaxPaymentDetails."Credit availed";
                                  CreditUsedForSTPmtECess := TotalServTaxPaymentDetails."Credit availed (eCess)";
                                  CreditUsedForSTPmtSHECess := TotalServTaxPaymentDetails."Credit availed (SHECess)";
                                  CreditUsedForSTPmtKKCess := TotalServTaxPaymentDetails."Credit Available (KKC)";


                                  CalcExcisePaidInPeriod(StartDate,EndDate,TotalSTAsExciseUtilization);
                                  CreditUsedForExcPmt := TotalSTAsExciseUtilization."ST as Excise Utilisation";
                                  CreditUsedForExcPmtECess := TotalSTAsExciseUtilization."ST eCess as Excise Utilisation";
                                  CreditUsedForExcPmtSHECess := TotalSTAsExciseUtilization."ST SHECess Excise Utilisation";

                                  // Totals
                                  TotalCreditAvailable := OpeningBalance + CreditAvailed;
                                  TotalCreditAvailableEcess := OpeningBalanceEcess + CreditAvailedECess;
                                  TotalCreditAvailableSHECess := OpeningBalanceSheCess + CreditAvailedSHECess;
                                  TotalCreditAvailableKKCess := OpeningBalanceKKCess + CreditAvailedKKCess ;
                                  CreditUsed := CreditUsedForSTPmt + CreditUsedForExcPmt;
                                  CreditUsedECess := CreditUsedForSTPmtECess + CreditUsedForExcPmtECess;
                                  CreditUsedSHECess := CreditUsedForSTPmtSHECess + CreditUsedForExcPmtSHECess;
                                  CreditUsedKKCess := CreditUsedForSTPmtKKCess;


                                  ClosingBalance := TotalCreditAvailable - CreditUsed;
                                  ClosingBalanceECess := TotalCreditAvailableEcess - CreditUsedECess;
                                  ClosingBalanceSHECess := TotalCreditAvailableSHECess - CreditUsedSHECess;
                                  ClosingBalanceKKCess :=  TotalCreditAvailableKKCess - CreditUsedKKCess;
                                END;
                                 }

    { 9889;1   ;DataItem;CrAvailedDetail     ;
               DataItemTable=Table2000000026;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(Number)
                                 ORDER(Ascending);
               OnPreDataItem=BEGIN
                               IF NOT Details OR STEntryDetails.ISEMPTY THEN
                                 CurrReport.BREAK;

                               SETRANGE(Number,1,STEntryDetails.COUNT);
                               CurrReport.CREATETOTALS(
                                 STEntryDetails.Amount,
                                 STEntryDetails."Service Tax Amount",
                                 STEntryDetails."Service Tax eCess Amount",
                                 STEntryDetails."Service Tax SHE Cess Amount",
                                 STEntryDetails."KK Cess Amount");
                             END;

               OnAfterGetRecord=VAR
                                  VendLedgEntry@1500002 : Record 25;
                                  ServiceTaxEntry@1500001 : Record 16473;
                                  State@1500000 : Record 13762;
                                BEGIN
                                  IF Number = 1 THEN
                                    STEntryDetails.FINDSET
                                  ELSE
                                    STEntryDetails.NEXT;

                                  ShowCrAvailedDetailBody3 := NOT STEntryDetails."ST Credit Received";
                                  ShowCrAvailedDetailBody4 := STEntryDetails."ST Credit Received";

                                  SrNo := SrNo + 1;

                                  IF ServiceTaxEntry.GET(STEntryDetails."Service Tax Entry No.") THEN;
                                  VendLedgEntry.SETCURRENTKEY("Transaction No.");
                                  VendLedgEntry.SETRANGE("Transaction No.",ServiceTaxEntry."Transaction No.");
                                  IF VendLedgEntry.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
                                    DocumentNo := VendLedgEntry."External Document No.";
                                    Vendor.GET(VendLedgEntry."Vendor No.");
                                  END ELSE
                                    IF STEntryDetails."ST Credit Received" THEN
                                      DocumentNo := STEntryDetails."Document No."
                                    ELSE
                                      DocumentNo := '';

                                  NameOfISD := '';
                                  IF STEntryDetails."ST Credit Received" THEN
                                    IF STEntryDetails."From Location" = '' THEN
                                      NameOfISD := CompanyInfo.Name + ' ' + CompanyInfo."Name 2"
                                    ELSE
                                      NameOfISD := STEntryDetails."From Location";

                                  VendorName := '';
                                  Address := '';
                                  IF STEntryDetails."From Location" <> '' THEN BEGIN
                                    Location.GET(STEntryDetails."From Location");
                                    IF State.GET(Location."State Code") THEN;
                                    Address := Location.Address + ',' + Location."Address 2" + ', ' + State.Description;
                                    ServiceTaxRegNo := Location."Service Tax Registration No.";
                                  END ELSE
                                    IF (STEntryDetails."From Location" = '') AND STEntryDetails."ST Credit Received" THEN BEGIN
                                      IF State.GET(CompanyInfo.State) THEN;
                                      Address := CompanyInfo.Address + ', ' + CompanyInfo."Address 2" + ', ' + State.Description;
                                      ServiceTaxRegNo := CompanyInfo."Service Tax Registration No.";
                                    END ELSE BEGIN
                                      IF State.GET(Vendor."State Code") THEN;
                                      Address := Vendor.Address + ', ' + Vendor."Address 2" + ', ' + State.Description;
                                      ServiceTaxRegNo := Vendor."Service Tax Registration No.";
                                      VendorName := Vendor.Name + ' ' + Vendor."Name 2";
                                    END;

                                  IF SvcTaxGroup.GET(STEntryDetails."Service Tax Group Code") THEN;

                                  IF STEntryDetails."ST Credit Received" THEN BEGIN
                                    STEntryDetails.Amount := 0;
                                    AmountPaid := 'N.A.';
                                  END;
                                  IF STEntryDetails."Reverse Charge" THEN
                                    STEntryDate := STEntryDetails."Payment Document Date"
                                  ELSE
                                    STEntryDate := STEntryDetails."Posting Date";
                                END;
                                 }

    { 3320;1   ;DataItem;CrUtilzedHeader     ;
               DataItemTable=Table2000000026;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(Number)
                                 ORDER(Ascending)
                                 WHERE(Number=CONST(1));
               OnPreDataItem=BEGIN
                               STPaymentDetails.SETCURRENTKEY("Posting Date","Document No.");
                               IF STPaymentDetails.FINDSET THEN
                                 REPEAT
                                   IF (STPaymentDetails."Credit availed" <> 0) OR (STPaymentDetails."Credit availed (eCess)" <> 0) OR
                                      (STPaymentDetails."Credit availed (SHECess)" <> 0) OR (STPaymentDetails."Credit Availed (KKC)" <> 0)
                                   THEN
                                     STPaymentDetails.MARK(TRUE);
                                 UNTIL STPaymentDetails.NEXT = 0;
                               STPaymentDetails.MARKEDONLY(TRUE);

                               CurrReport.BREAK;
                             END;
                              }

    { 1170000014;2;Column;CrUtilzedHeader_Number;

    PROCEDURE STAsExciseUtalization@1500015();
    BEGIN
      STasExciseUtilisation2.RESET;
      STasExciseUtilisation2.SETCURRENTKEY("Service Tax Registration No.","Posting Date","Document No.");
      STasExciseUtilisation2.SETRANGE("Document No.",STasExciseUtilisation."Document No.");
      STasExciseUtilisation2.CALCSUMS("ST as Excise Utilisation","ST eCess as Excise Utilisation","ST SHECess Excise Utilisation");
    END;

    PROCEDURE STPaymentDetail@1500003();
    BEGIN
      STPmtDetails.RESET;
      STPmtDetails.SETCURRENTKEY("Document No.","Challan No.");
      STPmtDetails.SETRANGE("Document No.",STPaymentDetails."Document No.");
      STPmtDetails.CALCSUMS("Credit availed","Credit availed (eCess)","Credit availed (SHECess)","Credit Availed (KKC)");
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE CalcTaxInPeriod@1500005(FromDate@1500000 : Date;ToDate@1500001 : Date;VAR TaxAmount@1500002 : Decimal;VAR ECessAmount@1500003 : Decimal;VAR SheCessAmount@1500004 : Decimal;VAR KKCessAmount@1500005 : Decimal);
    BEGIN
      MarkDetailsServTaxEntries(FromDate,ToDate,STEntryDetails);
      STEntryDetails.CALCSUMS("Service Tax Amount","Service Tax eCess Amount","Service Tax SHE Cess Amount");

      TaxAmount := STEntryDetails."Service Tax Amount";
      ECessAmount := STEntryDetails."Service Tax eCess Amount";
      SheCessAmount := STEntryDetails."Service Tax SHE Cess Amount";
      KKCessAmount := STEntryDetails."KK Cess Amount";
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE CalcTaxPaymentsInPeriod@1500008(FromDate@1500004 : Date;ToDate@1500003 : Date;VAR TotalServTaxPaymentDetails@1500005 : Record 16477);
    BEGIN
      STPaymentDetails.RESET;
      STPaymentDetails.SETCURRENTKEY("Service Tax Registration No.","Service Tax Group Code","Posting Date");
      STPaymentDetails.SETRANGE("Service Tax Registration No.",STRegistrationNo);
      STPaymentDetails.SETRANGE("Posting Date",FromDate,ToDate);
      STPaymentDetails.SETFILTER("Service Tax Group Code",'<>%1','');
      STPaymentDetails.CALCSUMS("Credit availed","Credit availed (eCess)","Credit availed (SHECess)","Credit Availed (KKC)");
      TotalServTaxPaymentDetails := STPaymentDetails;
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE CalcExcisePaidInPeriod@1500009(FromDate@1500004 : Date;ToDate@1500003 : Date;VAR TotalSTAsExciseUtilization@1500000 : Record 16570);
    BEGIN
      STasExciseUtilisation.RESET;
      STasExciseUtilisation.SETCURRENTKEY("Service Tax Registration No.","Posting Date");
      STasExciseUtilisation.SETRANGE("Service Tax Registration No.",STRegistrationNo);
      STasExciseUtilisation.SETRANGE("Posting Date",FromDate,ToDate);
      STasExciseUtilisation.CALCSUMS("ST as Excise Utilisation","ST eCess as Excise Utilisation","ST SHECess Excise Utilisation");
      TotalSTAsExciseUtilization := STasExciseUtilisation;
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE MarkDetailsServTaxEntries@1500011(FromDate@1500001 : Date;ToDate@1500002 : Date;VAR ServiceTaxEntryDetails@1500000 : Record 16474);
    BEGIN
      WITH ServiceTaxEntryDetails DO BEGIN
        // All non-Reverse Charge
        RESET;
        SETCURRENTKEY(
          Type,"Service Tax Registration No.","Service Tax Group Code","Posting Date","Input Service Distribution");
        SETRANGE(Type,Type::Purchase);
        SETRANGE("Service Tax Registration No.",STRegistrationNo);
        SETRANGE("Posting Date",FromDate,ToDate);
        SETRANGE("Input Service Distribution",FALSE);
        SETRANGE("Zero Amount",FALSE);
        SETFILTER("Service Type (Rev. Chrg.)",'<>%1',"Service Type (Rev. Chrg.)"::Outward);
        SETRANGE("Reverse Charge",FALSE);
        IF FINDSET THEN
          REPEAT
            MARK(TRUE);
          UNTIL NEXT = 0;

        // Paid Reverse Charge
        SETRANGE("Posting Date");
        SETRANGE("Reverse Charge",TRUE);
        SETFILTER("Reverse Charge Pmt. Doc. No.",'<>%1','');
        SETRANGE("Payment Document Date",FromDate,ToDate);
        IF FINDSET THEN
          REPEAT
            MARK(TRUE);
          UNTIL NEXT = 0;

        SETRANGE("Reverse Charge");
        SETRANGE("Reverse Charge Pmt. Doc. No.");
        SETRANGE("Payment Document Date");

        MARKEDONLY(TRUE);
      END;
    END;

    BEGIN
    END.
  }

  <Code>Public Function BlankZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value = 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &gt; 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankZeroAndPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &gt;= 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNeg(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &lt; 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNegAndZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &lt;= 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Shared Data As String
Public Function SetData(ByVal Value As String)
    if Value &lt;&gt; "" then
        Data = Value
    end if
    Return True
End Function

Public Function GetData(ByVal Num As Integer)
    Return Choose(Num, Split(Data,Chr(177)))
End Function</Code>
